6584 \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MUTEX_gaa6c9d809037676d22aceaf5517a33faf}{options} & (\hyperlink{pcre_8h_ac4743871720886cdb063a9102f18bf0a}{PCRE\_BSR\_ANYCRLF}|\hyperlink{pcre_8h_ac26454ae13931ee0bb369dff27b7c1e2}{PCRE\_BSR\_UNICODE}))
6585   \{
6586   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0:
6587   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((re->options & (\hyperlink{pcre_8h_ac4743871720886cdb063a9102f18bf0a}{PCRE\_BSR\_ANYCRLF}|\hyperlink{pcre_8h_ac26454ae13931ee0bb369dff27b7c1e2}{PCRE\_BSR\_UNICODE})) != 0)
6588     md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a1e4ff67dfc4a62b545e4502bdbc8b6d5}{bsr\_anycrlf} = (re->options & \hyperlink{pcre_8h_ac4743871720886cdb063a9102f18bf0a}{PCRE\_BSR\_ANYCRLF}) != 0;
6589   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
6590 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifdef BSR\_ANYCRLF}
6591   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a1e4ff67dfc4a62b545e4502bdbc8b6d5}{bsr\_anycrlf} = \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa8cecfc5c5c054d2875c03e77b7be15d}{TRUE};
6592 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#else}
6593   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a1e4ff67dfc4a62b545e4502bdbc8b6d5}{bsr\_anycrlf} = \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa93f0eb578d23995850d61f7d61c55c1}{FALSE};
6594 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
6595   \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6596 
6597   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_ac4743871720886cdb063a9102f18bf0a}{PCRE\_BSR\_ANYCRLF}:
6598   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a1e4ff67dfc4a62b545e4502bdbc8b6d5}{bsr\_anycrlf} = \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa8cecfc5c5c054d2875c03e77b7be15d}{TRUE};
6599   \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6600 
6601   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_ac26454ae13931ee0bb369dff27b7c1e2}{PCRE\_BSR\_UNICODE}:
6602   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a1e4ff67dfc4a62b545e4502bdbc8b6d5}{bsr\_anycrlf} = \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa93f0eb578d23995850d61f7d61c55c1}{FALSE};
6603   \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6604 
6605   \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_a1e5c85bff0f0ab4ec3b7da4eedc1c1dd}{PCRE\_ERROR\_BADNEWLINE};
6606   \}
6607 
6608 \textcolor{comment}{/* Handle different types of newline. The three bits give eight cases. If}
6609 \textcolor{comment}{nothing is set at run time, whatever was used at compile time applies. */}
6610 
6611 \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} ((((\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MUTEX_gaa6c9d809037676d22aceaf5517a33faf}{options} & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a3ee8247993b3ece18a68631e54007555}{PCRE\_NEWLINE\_BITS}) == 0)? re->options :
6612         (pcre\_uint32)\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MUTEX_gaa6c9d809037676d22aceaf5517a33faf}{options}) & PCRE\_NEWLINE\_BITS)
6613   \{
6614   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0: newline = \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_ab26dfb3784697f4ae91f356713845063}{NEWLINE}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};   \textcolor{comment}{/* Compile-time default */}
6615   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_ab55198e91574a143392a8dced9d5cf85}{PCRE\_NEWLINE\_CR}: newline = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a96f70aecaff003e01fc8bcf2f070c5ef}{CHAR\_CR}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6616   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_a9d3e03ae881322fe05e72e7ad111bf4f}{PCRE\_NEWLINE\_LF}: newline = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a8edcdaf0b586f0ad461b6e7aced9ba09}{CHAR\_NL}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6617   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_ab55198e91574a143392a8dced9d5cf85}{PCRE\_NEWLINE\_CR}+
6618        \hyperlink{pcre_8h_a9d3e03ae881322fe05e72e7ad111bf4f}{PCRE\_NEWLINE\_LF}: newline = (\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a96f70aecaff003e01fc8bcf2f070c5ef}{CHAR\_CR} << 8) | \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a8edcdaf0b586f0ad461b6e7aced9ba09}{CHAR\_NL}; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6619   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_a1c379cd4b51ea037dce7e8c79f9ee57d}{PCRE\_NEWLINE\_ANY}: newline = -1; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6620   \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_af25f19586bec4187ca77e617ddc9b98b}{PCRE\_NEWLINE\_ANYCRLF}: newline = -2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6621   \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}: \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_a1e5c85bff0f0ab4ec3b7da4eedc1c1dd}{PCRE\_ERROR\_BADNEWLINE};
6622   \}
6623 
6624 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (newline == -2)
6625   \{
6626   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a2633f641c966b838ce255ce6da811fb1}{nltype} = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a27a269d5670306a753a98413273ea9be}{NLTYPE\_ANYCRLF};
6627   \}
6628 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (newline < 0)
6629   \{
6630   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a2633f641c966b838ce255ce6da811fb1}{nltype} = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_acf7dfdf7c85c3d4a4db4d2d3547611d2}{NLTYPE\_ANY};
6631   \}
6632 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
6633   \{
6634   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a2633f641c966b838ce255ce6da811fb1}{nltype} = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a479214957206efe3295aba2dbfb35a9c}{NLTYPE\_FIXED};
6635   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (newline > 255)
6636     \{
6637     md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a492828201e679386f5f172ff696522b4}{nllen} = 2;
6638     md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a18efae84ab8fb1b77c170c301d880f0f}{nl}[0] = (newline >> 8) & 255;
6639     md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a18efae84ab8fb1b77c170c301d880f0f}{nl}[1] = newline & 255;
6640     \}
6641   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
6642     \{
6643     md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a492828201e679386f5f172ff696522b4}{nllen} = 1;
6644     md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a18efae84ab8fb1b77c170c301d880f0f}{nl}[0] = \hyperlink{NON-AUTOTOOLS-BUILD_8txt_a9f48ea6b13757e0a4c5b5a6dfd7f178e}{newline};
6645     \}
6646   \}
6647 
6648 \textcolor{comment}{/* Partial matching was originally supported only for a restricted set of}
6649 \textcolor{comment}{regexes; from release 8.00 there are no restrictions, but the bits are still}
6650 \textcolor{comment}{defined (though never set). So there's no harm in leaving this code. */}
6651 
6652 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a43d3a8b23fca5e166e86b27f3df0033a}{partial} && (re->flags & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a7eada40373dcbebeba6d3d984530fa51}{PCRE\_NOPARTIAL}) != 0)
6653   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_af26f30ebc125fbd27b82f49c2766740b}{PCRE\_ERROR\_BADPARTIAL};
6654 
6655 \textcolor{comment}{/* If the expression has got more back references than the offsets supplied can}
6656 \textcolor{comment}{hold, we get a temporary chunk of working store to use during the matching.}
6657 \textcolor{comment}{Otherwise, we can use the vector supplied, rounding down its size to a multiple}
6658 \textcolor{comment}{of 3. */}
6659 
6660 ocount = offsetcount - (offsetcount % 3);
6661 arg\_offset\_max = (2*ocount)/3;
6662 
6663 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (re->top\_backref > 0 && re->top\_backref >= ocount/3)
6664   \{
6665   ocount = re->top\_backref * 3 + 3;
6666   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector} = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *)(\hyperlink{pcre__globals_8c_af69d8e852882cfd50b98c0481ba3b98a}{PUBL}(\hyperlink{util__expr__parse_8c_a5faf6a2d99f50a4655dd390199a8db7b}{malloc}))(ocount * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}));
6667   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector} == \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL}) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{pcre_8h_ac6c7a9107b8a1a8616f824fb30a3569a}{PCRE\_ERROR\_NOMEMORY};
6668   using\_temporary\_offsets = \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa8cecfc5c5c054d2875c03e77b7be15d}{TRUE};
6669   \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a927243fe3d588e31de3f3badd5c47d47}{DPRINTF}((\textcolor{stringliteral}{"Got memory to hold back references\(\backslash\)n"}));
6670   \}
6671 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector} = \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_afeda8db30b411d6c918c917b867d0309}{offsets};
6672 md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a39b086546dc588e6dc2f3af1a82b9313}{offset\_end} = ocount;
6673 md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a93ffc54250bf51f1e979becfa68c7fc2}{offset\_max} = (2*ocount)/3;
6674 md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a141305fd6175f338a8718fa883f5b672}{capture\_last} = 0;
6675 
6676 \textcolor{comment}{/* Reset the working variable associated with each extraction. These should}
6677 \textcolor{comment}{never be used unless previously set, but they get saved and restored, and so we}
6678 \textcolor{comment}{initialize them to avoid reading uninitialized locations. Also, unset the}
6679 \textcolor{comment}{offsets for the matched string. This is really just for tidiness with callouts,}
6680 \textcolor{comment}{in case they inspect these fields. */}
6681 
6682 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector} != \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL})
6683   \{
6684   \textcolor{keyword}{register} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *iptr = md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector} + ocount;
6685   \textcolor{keyword}{register} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *iend = iptr - re->top\_bracket;
6686   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (iend < md->offset\_vector + 2) iend = md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector} + 2;
6687   \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (--iptr >= iend) *iptr = -1;
6688   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (offsetcount > 0) md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector}[0] = -1;
6689   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (offsetcount > 1) md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector}[1] = -1;
6690   \}
6691 
6692 \textcolor{comment}{/* Set up the first character to match, if available. The first\_char value is}
6693 \textcolor{comment}{never set for an anchored regular expression, but the anchoring may be forced}
6694 \textcolor{comment}{at run time, so we have to test for anchoring. The first char may be unset for}
6695 \textcolor{comment}{an unanchored pattern, of course. If there's no first char and the pattern was}
6696 \textcolor{comment}{studied, there may be a bitmap of possible first characters. */}
6697 
6698 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!anchored)
6699   \{
6700   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((re->flags & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aa3860b4c31ee4275eaa19df78bc73590}{PCRE\_FIRSTSET}) != 0)
6701     \{
6702     has\_first\_char = \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa8cecfc5c5c054d2875c03e77b7be15d}{TRUE};
6703     first\_char = first\_char2 = (\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a9d8efd0ad5b191db2a1793268600deb9}{pcre\_uchar})(re->first\_char);
6704     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((re->flags & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a91834d023916ad826da8eb6bbb316863}{PCRE\_FCH\_CASELESS}) != 0)
6705       \{
6706       first\_char2 = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aa84187a7859fca5852603b35325b553f}{TABLE\_GET}(first\_char, md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_accda5269f5b22cf383425cde86bf25af}{fcc}, first\_char);
6707 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if defined SUPPORT\_UCP && !(defined COMPILE\_PCRE8)}
6708       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (utf && first\_char > 127)
6709         first\_char2 = UCD\_OTHERCASE(first\_char);
6710 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
6711       \}
6712     \}
6713   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
6714     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (!startline && study != \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL} &&
6715       (study->\hyperlink{structpcre__study__data_aa7f0cd71352343074202364478c25a4d}{flags} & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a4bbaa1bde305f5aa75950082a6fa8870}{PCRE\_STUDY\_MAPPED}) != 0)
6716         start\_bits = study->\hyperlink{structpcre__study__data_ab4dd0613033fa41c5cd084a98b4c0fb0}{start\_bits};
6717   \}
6718 
6719 \textcolor{comment}{/* For anchored or unanchored matches, there may be a "last known required}
6720 \textcolor{comment}{character" set. */}
6721 
6722 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((re->flags & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a6c85b22f5b731db51da6177b20aa0ebd}{PCRE\_REQCHSET}) != 0)
6723   \{
6724   has\_req\_char = \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa8cecfc5c5c054d2875c03e77b7be15d}{TRUE};
6725   req\_char = req\_char2 = (\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a9d8efd0ad5b191db2a1793268600deb9}{pcre\_uchar})(re->req\_char);
6726   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((re->flags & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aabd065c48c6bc64165e21d664e17f27f}{PCRE\_RCH\_CASELESS}) != 0)
6727     \{
6728     req\_char2 = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aa84187a7859fca5852603b35325b553f}{TABLE\_GET}(req\_char, md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_accda5269f5b22cf383425cde86bf25af}{fcc}, req\_char);
6729 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if defined SUPPORT\_UCP && !(defined COMPILE\_PCRE8)}
6730     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (utf && req\_char > 127)
6731       req\_char2 = UCD\_OTHERCASE(req\_char);
6732 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
6733     \}
6734   \}
6735 
6736 
6737 \textcolor{comment}{/* ==========================================================================*/}
6738 
6739 \textcolor{comment}{/* Loop for handling unanchored repeated matching attempts; for anchored regexs}
6740 \textcolor{comment}{the loop runs just once. */}
6741 
6742 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for}(;;)
6743   \{
6744   \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a142c7c692c1f94083b0ad52e0520e900}{PCRE\_PUCHAR} save\_end\_subject = end\_subject;
6745   \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a142c7c692c1f94083b0ad52e0520e900}{PCRE\_PUCHAR} new\_start\_match;
6746 
6747   \textcolor{comment}{/* If firstline is TRUE, the start of the match is constrained to the first}
6748 \textcolor{comment}{  line of a multiline string. That is, the match must be before or at the first}
6749 \textcolor{comment}{  newline. Implement this by temporarily adjusting end\_subject so that we stop}
6750 \textcolor{comment}{  scanning at a newline. If the match fails at the newline, later code breaks}
6751 \textcolor{comment}{  this loop. */}
6752 
6753   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (firstline)
6754     \{
6755     \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a142c7c692c1f94083b0ad52e0520e900}{PCRE\_PUCHAR} \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__DAEMON_gabfa74bb4f05f3b2de1a89160025e5400}{t} = start\_match;
6756 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifdef SUPPORT\_UTF}
6757     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (utf)
6758       \{
6759       \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (t < md->end\_subject && !\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aa2114a8b1a4144413857626d01cee5d8}{IS\_NEWLINE}(t))
6760         \{
6761         t++;
6762         ACROSSCHAR(t < end\_subject, *t, t++);
6763         \}
6764       \}
6765     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
6766 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
6767     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (t < md->end\_subject && !\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aa2114a8b1a4144413857626d01cee5d8}{IS\_NEWLINE}(t)) t++;
6768     end\_subject = \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__DAEMON_gabfa74bb4f05f3b2de1a89160025e5400}{t};
6769     \}
6770 
6771   \textcolor{comment}{/* There are some optimizations that avoid running the match if a known}
6772 \textcolor{comment}{  starting point is not found, or if a known later character is not present.}
6773 \textcolor{comment}{  However, there is an option that disables these, for testing and for ensuring}
6774 \textcolor{comment}{  that all callouts do actually occur. The option can be set in the regex by}
6775 \textcolor{comment}{  (*NO\_START\_OPT) or passed in match-time options. */}
6776 
6777   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (((\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MUTEX_gaa6c9d809037676d22aceaf5517a33faf}{options} | re->options) & \hyperlink{pcre_8h_ab07c8c2c3a7fc070d2da0ec9bdf8a873}{PCRE\_NO\_START\_OPTIMIZE}) == 0)
6778     \{
6779     \textcolor{comment}{/* Advance to a unique first char if there is one. */}
6780 
6781     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (has\_first\_char)
6782       \{
6783       \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a9d8efd0ad5b191db2a1793268600deb9}{pcre\_uchar} smc;
6784 
6785       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (first\_char != first\_char2)
6786         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (start\_match < end\_subject &&
6787           (smc = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a7d99cf70792624c2ecda69a30006b1fa}{UCHAR21TEST}(start\_match)) != first\_char && smc != first\_char2)
6788           start\_match++;
6789       \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
6790         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (start\_match < end\_subject && \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a7d99cf70792624c2ecda69a30006b1fa}{UCHAR21TEST}(start\_match) != first\_char)
6791           start\_match++;
6792       \}
6793 
6794     \textcolor{comment}{/* Or to just after a linebreak for a multiline match */}
6795 
6796     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (startline)
6797       \{
6798       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (start\_match > md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a463372ba613f0f74066c89590b55f35e}{start\_subject} + start\_offset)
6799         \{
6800 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifdef SUPPORT\_UTF}
6801         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (utf)
6802           \{
6803           \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (start\_match < end\_subject && !\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_ab6d8d1affa9e7b200180e789bad9b9cd}{WAS\_NEWLINE}(start\_match))
6804             \{
6805             start\_match++;
6806             ACROSSCHAR(start\_match < end\_subject, *start\_match,
6807               start\_match++);
6808             \}
6809           \}
6810         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
6811 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
6812         \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (start\_match < end\_subject && !\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_ab6d8d1affa9e7b200180e789bad9b9cd}{WAS\_NEWLINE}(start\_match))
6813           start\_match++;
6814 
6815         \textcolor{comment}{/* If we have just passed a CR and the newline option is ANY or ANYCRLF,}
6816 \textcolor{comment}{        and we are now at a LF, advance the match position by one more character.}
6817 \textcolor{comment}{        */}
6818 
6819         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (start\_match[-1] == \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a96f70aecaff003e01fc8bcf2f070c5ef}{CHAR\_CR} &&
6820              (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a2633f641c966b838ce255ce6da811fb1}{nltype} == \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_acf7dfdf7c85c3d4a4db4d2d3547611d2}{NLTYPE\_ANY} || md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a2633f641c966b838ce255ce6da811fb1}{nltype} == 
      \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a27a269d5670306a753a98413273ea9be}{NLTYPE\_ANYCRLF}) &&
6821              start\_match < end\_subject &&
6822              \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a7d99cf70792624c2ecda69a30006b1fa}{UCHAR21TEST}(start\_match) == \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a8edcdaf0b586f0ad461b6e7aced9ba09}{CHAR\_NL})
6823           start\_match++;
6824         \}
6825       \}
6826 
6827     \textcolor{comment}{/* Or to a non-unique first byte after study */}
6828 
6829     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (start\_bits != \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL})
6830       \{
6831       \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (start\_match < end\_subject)
6832         \{
6833         \textcolor{keyword}{register} pcre\_uint32 \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__HTTPD_ga7cce37ef8558e46f408cb4d0f555605b}{c} = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a7d99cf70792624c2ecda69a30006b1fa}{UCHAR21TEST}(start\_match);
6834 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifndef COMPILE\_PCRE8}
6835         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (c > 255) c = 255;
6836 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
6837         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((start\_bits[c/8] & (1 << (c&7))) != 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6838         start\_match++;
6839         \}
6840       \}
6841     \}   \textcolor{comment}{/* Starting optimizations */}
6842 
6843   \textcolor{comment}{/* Restore fudged end\_subject */}
6844 
6845   end\_subject = save\_end\_subject;
6846 
6847   \textcolor{comment}{/* The following two optimizations are disabled for partial matching or if}
6848 \textcolor{comment}{  disabling is explicitly requested. */}
6849 
6850   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (((\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MUTEX_gaa6c9d809037676d22aceaf5517a33faf}{options} | re->options) & \hyperlink{pcre_8h_ab07c8c2c3a7fc070d2da0ec9bdf8a873}{PCRE\_NO\_START\_OPTIMIZE}) == 0 && !md->
      \hyperlink{structmatch__data_a43d3a8b23fca5e166e86b27f3df0033a}{partial})
6851     \{
6852     \textcolor{comment}{/* If the pattern was studied, a minimum subject length may be set. This is}
6853 \textcolor{comment}{    a lower bound; no actual string of that length may actually match the}
6854 \textcolor{comment}{    pattern. Although the value is, strictly, in characters, we treat it as}
6855 \textcolor{comment}{    bytes to avoid spending too much time in this optimization. */}
6856 
6857     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (study != \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL} && (study->\hyperlink{structpcre__study__data_aa7f0cd71352343074202364478c25a4d}{flags} & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a99cb4a3ffaa73a220e660acb23c749c4}{PCRE\_STUDY\_MINLEN}) != 0 &&
6858         (pcre\_uint32)(end\_subject - start\_match) < study->\hyperlink{structpcre__study__data_a50cb4fc8a227db9bfe3568764aca3274}{minlength})
6859       \{
6860       rc = \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_aca955f0e1e921adb03901b56eeff3da0}{MATCH\_NOMATCH};
6861       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6862       \}
6863 
6864     \textcolor{comment}{/* If req\_char is set, we know that that character must appear in the}
6865 \textcolor{comment}{    subject for the match to succeed. If the first character is set, req\_char}
6866 \textcolor{comment}{    must be later in the subject; otherwise the test starts at the match point.}
6867 \textcolor{comment}{    This optimization can save a huge amount of backtracking in patterns with}
6868 \textcolor{comment}{    nested unlimited repeats that aren't going to match. Writing separate code}
6869 \textcolor{comment}{    for cased/caseless versions makes it go faster, as does using an}
6870 \textcolor{comment}{    autoincrement and backing off on a match.}
6871 \textcolor{comment}{}
6872 \textcolor{comment}{    HOWEVER: when the subject string is very, very long, searching to its end}
6873 \textcolor{comment}{    can take a long time, and give bad performance on quite ordinary patterns.}
6874 \textcolor{comment}{    This showed up when somebody was matching something like /^\(\backslash\)d+C/ on a}
6875 \textcolor{comment}{    32-megabyte string... so we don't do this when the string is sufficiently}
6876 \textcolor{comment}{    long. */}
6877 
6878     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (has\_req\_char && end\_subject - start\_match < \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a2a71b1d448dc7433849f0f7cc0770c4b}{REQ\_BYTE\_MAX})
6879       \{
6880       \textcolor{keyword}{register} \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a142c7c692c1f94083b0ad52e0520e900}{PCRE\_PUCHAR} \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MPM_ga5cd91701e5c167f2b1a38e70ab57817e}{p} = start\_match + (has\_first\_char? 1:0);
6881 
6882       \textcolor{comment}{/* We don't need to repeat the search if we haven't yet reached the}
6883 \textcolor{comment}{      place we found it at last time. */}
6884 
6885       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (p > req\_char\_ptr)
6886         \{
6887         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (req\_char != req\_char2)
6888           \{
6889           \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (p < end\_subject)
6890             \{
6891             \textcolor{keyword}{register} pcre\_uint32 pp = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aadfae2f5e97656be522818f4ef22bd51}{UCHAR21INCTEST}(p);
6892             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (pp == req\_char || pp == req\_char2) \{ p--; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break}; \}
6893             \}
6894           \}
6895         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
6896           \{
6897           \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (p < end\_subject)
6898             \{
6899             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aadfae2f5e97656be522818f4ef22bd51}{UCHAR21INCTEST}(p) == req\_char) \{ p--; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break}; \}
6900             \}
6901           \}
6902 
6903         \textcolor{comment}{/* If we can't find the required character, break the matching loop,}
6904 \textcolor{comment}{        forcing a match failure. */}
6905 
6906         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (p >= end\_subject)
6907           \{
6908           rc = \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_aca955f0e1e921adb03901b56eeff3da0}{MATCH\_NOMATCH};
6909           \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6910           \}
6911 
6912         \textcolor{comment}{/* If we have found the required character, save the point where we}
6913 \textcolor{comment}{        found it, so that we don't search again next time round the loop if}
6914 \textcolor{comment}{        the start hasn't passed this character yet. */}
6915 
6916         req\_char\_ptr = \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MPM_ga5cd91701e5c167f2b1a38e70ab57817e}{p};
6917         \}
6918       \}
6919     \}
6920 
6921 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifdef PCRE\_DEBUG  }\textcolor{comment}{/* Sigh. Some compilers never learn. */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}
6922   printf(\textcolor{stringliteral}{">>>> Match against: "});
6923   pchars(start\_match, end\_subject - start\_match, \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa8cecfc5c5c054d2875c03e77b7be15d}{TRUE}, md);
6924   printf(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"\(\backslash\)n"});
6925 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
6926 
6927   \textcolor{comment}{/* OK, we can now run the match. If "hitend" is set afterwards, remember the}
6928 \textcolor{comment}{  first starting point for which a partial match was found. */}
6929 
6930   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a169aeb315352d6fffadb69076e89feff}{start\_match\_ptr} = start\_match;
6931   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a40b57f042d200e27b92051307f6d3b64}{start\_used\_ptr} = start\_match;
6932   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a5e6bd79005e22ca77960df0d6a31c462}{match\_call\_count} = 0;
6933   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_af32d7c84dc11582bf594a02058c4dd87}{match\_function\_type} = 0;
6934   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a6befbc845fc277e998e3a29ec7868049}{end\_offset\_top} = 0;
6935   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a349f6b34f861a9873e653d70e2998c42}{skip\_arg\_count} = 0;
6936   rc = \hyperlink{ap__regex_8h_a543b7bf3899cd49d687c072cb0124ea9}{match}(start\_match, md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a3472db3871acca036227d544aba94267}{start\_code}, start\_match, 2, md, 
      \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL}, 0);
6937   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a3666025c6e56a8a56052d3aed5effe41}{hitend} && start\_partial == \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL})
6938     \{
6939     start\_partial = md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a40b57f042d200e27b92051307f6d3b64}{start\_used\_ptr};
6940     match\_partial = start\_match;
6941     \}
6942 
6943   \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch}(rc)
6944     \{
6945     \textcolor{comment}{/* If MATCH\_SKIP\_ARG reaches this level it means that a MARK that matched}
6946 \textcolor{comment}{    the SKIP's arg was not found. In this circumstance, Perl ignores the SKIP}
6947 \textcolor{comment}{    entirely. The only way we can do that is to re-do the match at the same}
6948 \textcolor{comment}{    point, with a flag to force SKIP with an argument to be ignored. Just}
6949 \textcolor{comment}{    treating this case as NOMATCH does not work because it does not check other}
6950 \textcolor{comment}{    alternatives in patterns such as A(*SKIP:A)B|AC when the subject is AC. */}
6951 
6952     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_a555b2c319d93783559c5059be91ca4ca}{MATCH\_SKIP\_ARG}:
6953     new\_start\_match = start\_match;
6954     md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a36d4f1f1f33dd2484bc545514a3eccfe}{ignore\_skip\_arg} = md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a349f6b34f861a9873e653d70e2998c42}{skip\_arg\_count};
6955     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6956 
6957     \textcolor{comment}{/* SKIP passes back the next starting point explicitly, but if it is no}
6958 \textcolor{comment}{    greater than the match we have just done, treat it as NOMATCH. */}
6959 
6960     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_acbc0f7566eeabbac89fe5b89717de268}{MATCH\_SKIP}:
6961     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a169aeb315352d6fffadb69076e89feff}{start\_match\_ptr} > start\_match)
6962       \{
6963       new\_start\_match = md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a169aeb315352d6fffadb69076e89feff}{start\_match\_ptr};
6964       \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6965       \}
6966     \textcolor{comment}{/* Fall through */}
6967 
6968     \textcolor{comment}{/* NOMATCH and PRUNE advance by one character. THEN at this level acts}
6969 \textcolor{comment}{    exactly like PRUNE. Unset ignore SKIP-with-argument. */}
6970 
6971     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_aca955f0e1e921adb03901b56eeff3da0}{MATCH\_NOMATCH}:
6972     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_ae6e9fd641ed9b6935df84b93be751bec}{MATCH\_PRUNE}:
6973     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_afae773c66af7140c59d08497327b3ac2}{MATCH\_THEN}:
6974     md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a36d4f1f1f33dd2484bc545514a3eccfe}{ignore\_skip\_arg} = 0;
6975     new\_start\_match = start\_match + 1;
6976 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifdef SUPPORT\_UTF}
6977     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (utf)
6978       ACROSSCHAR(new\_start\_match < end\_subject, *new\_start\_match,
6979         new\_start\_match++);
6980 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
6981     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
6982 
6983     \textcolor{comment}{/* COMMIT disables the bumpalong, but otherwise behaves as NOMATCH. */}
6984 
6985     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_a560d9767207605c03f77b9ad8850b000}{MATCH\_COMMIT}:
6986     rc = \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_aca955f0e1e921adb03901b56eeff3da0}{MATCH\_NOMATCH};
6987     \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} ENDLOOP;
6988 
6989     \textcolor{comment}{/* Any other return is either a match, or some kind of error. */}
6990 
6991     \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:
6992     \textcolor{keywordflow}{goto} ENDLOOP;
6993     \}
6994 
6995   \textcolor{comment}{/* Control reaches here for the various types of "no match at this point"}
6996 \textcolor{comment}{  result. Reset the code to MATCH\_NOMATCH for subsequent checking. */}
6997 
6998   rc = \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_aca955f0e1e921adb03901b56eeff3da0}{MATCH\_NOMATCH};
6999 
7000   \textcolor{comment}{/* If PCRE\_FIRSTLINE is set, the match must happen before or at the first}
7001 \textcolor{comment}{  newline in the subject (though it may continue over the newline). Therefore,}
7002 \textcolor{comment}{  if we have just failed to match, starting at a newline, do not continue. */}
7003 
7004   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (firstline && \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_aa2114a8b1a4144413857626d01cee5d8}{IS\_NEWLINE}(start\_match)) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
7005 
7006   \textcolor{comment}{/* Advance to new matching position */}
7007 
7008   start\_match = new\_start\_match;
7009 
7010   \textcolor{comment}{/* Break the loop if the pattern is anchored or if we have passed the end of}
7011 \textcolor{comment}{  the subject. */}
7012 
7013   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (anchored || start\_match > end\_subject) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
7014 
7015   \textcolor{comment}{/* If we have just passed a CR and we are now at a LF, and the pattern does}
7016 \textcolor{comment}{  not contain any explicit matches for \(\backslash\)r or \(\backslash\)n, and the newline option is CRLF}
7017 \textcolor{comment}{  or ANY or ANYCRLF, advance the match position by one more character. In}
7018 \textcolor{comment}{  normal matching start\_match will aways be greater than the first position at}
7019 \textcolor{comment}{  this stage, but a failed *SKIP can cause a return at the same point, which is}
7020 \textcolor{comment}{  why the first test exists. */}
7021 
7022   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (start\_match > (\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a142c7c692c1f94083b0ad52e0520e900}{PCRE\_PUCHAR})subject + start\_offset &&
7023       start\_match[-1] == \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a96f70aecaff003e01fc8bcf2f070c5ef}{CHAR\_CR} &&
7024       start\_match < end\_subject &&
7025       *start\_match == \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a8edcdaf0b586f0ad461b6e7aced9ba09}{CHAR\_NL} &&
7026       (re->flags & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a812a945823796f9a6db7bd05bda219e7}{PCRE\_HASCRORLF}) == 0 &&
7027         (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a2633f641c966b838ce255ce6da811fb1}{nltype} == \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_acf7dfdf7c85c3d4a4db4d2d3547611d2}{NLTYPE\_ANY} ||
7028          md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a2633f641c966b838ce255ce6da811fb1}{nltype} == \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a27a269d5670306a753a98413273ea9be}{NLTYPE\_ANYCRLF} ||
7029          md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a492828201e679386f5f172ff696522b4}{nllen} == 2))
7030     start\_match++;
7031 
7032   md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a393cc0e49b39ee0cb7c64ec248985a03}{mark} = \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL};   \textcolor{comment}{/* Reset for start of next match attempt */}
7033   \}                  \textcolor{comment}{/* End of for(;;) "bumpalong" loop */}
7034 
7035 \textcolor{comment}{/* ==========================================================================*/}
7036 
7037 \textcolor{comment}{/* We reach here when rc is not MATCH\_NOMATCH, or if one of the stopping}
7038 \textcolor{comment}{conditions is true:}
7039 \textcolor{comment}{}
7040 \textcolor{comment}{(1) The pattern is anchored or the match was failed by (*COMMIT);}
7041 \textcolor{comment}{}
7042 \textcolor{comment}{(2) We are past the end of the subject;}
7043 \textcolor{comment}{}
7044 \textcolor{comment}{(3) PCRE\_FIRSTLINE is set and we have failed to match at a newline, because}
7045 \textcolor{comment}{    this option requests that a match occur at or before the first newline in}
7046 \textcolor{comment}{    the subject.}
7047 \textcolor{comment}{}
7048 \textcolor{comment}{When we have a match and the offset vector is big enough to deal with any}
7049 \textcolor{comment}{backreferences, captured substring offsets will already be set up. In the case}
7050 \textcolor{comment}{where we had to get some local store to hold offsets for backreference}
7051 \textcolor{comment}{processing, copy those that we can. In this case there need not be overflow if}
7052 \textcolor{comment}{certain parts of the pattern were not used, even though there are more}
7053 \textcolor{comment}{capturing parentheses than vector slots. */}
7054 
7055 ENDLOOP:
7056 
7057 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rc == \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_a839e9651add1a00a00605a0b1b821a5b}{MATCH\_MATCH} || rc == \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_a4b41d08e1d62e96de3b44049a63cf76f}{MATCH\_ACCEPT})
7058   \{
7059   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (using\_temporary\_offsets)
7060     \{
7061     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (arg\_offset\_max >= 4)
7062       \{
7063       memcpy(\hyperlink{pcre_8txt_afeda8db30b411d6c918c917b867d0309}{offsets} + 2, md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector} + 2,
7064         (arg\_offset\_max - 2) * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int}));
7065       \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a927243fe3d588e31de3f3badd5c47d47}{DPRINTF}((\textcolor{stringliteral}{"Copied offsets from temporary memory\(\backslash\)n"}));
7066       \}
7067     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a6befbc845fc277e998e3a29ec7868049}{end\_offset\_top} > arg\_offset\_max) md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a141305fd6175f338a8718fa883f5b672}{capture\_last} |= 
      \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_af615a24ad764c30d37f5233ace00cd61}{OVFLBIT};
7068     \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a927243fe3d588e31de3f3badd5c47d47}{DPRINTF}((\textcolor{stringliteral}{"Freeing temporary memory\(\backslash\)n"}));
7069     (\hyperlink{pcre__globals_8c_af69d8e852882cfd50b98c0481ba3b98a}{PUBL}(\hyperlink{util__expr__parse_8c_af07d89f5ceaea0c7c8252cc41fd75f37}{free}))(md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a42ec3cf532803173d59637f9459637c0}{offset\_vector});
7070     \}
7071 
7072   \textcolor{comment}{/* Set the return code to the number of captured strings, or 0 if there were}
7073 \textcolor{comment}{  too many to fit into the vector. */}
7074 
7075   rc = ((md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a141305fd6175f338a8718fa883f5b672}{capture\_last} & \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_af615a24ad764c30d37f5233ace00cd61}{OVFLBIT}) != 0 &&
7076          md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a6befbc845fc277e998e3a29ec7868049}{end\_offset\_top} >= arg\_offset\_max)?
7077     0 : md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a6befbc845fc277e998e3a29ec7868049}{end\_offset\_top}/2;
7078 
7079   \textcolor{comment}{/* If there is space in the offset vector, set any unused pairs at the end of}
7080 \textcolor{comment}{  the pattern to -1 for backwards compatibility. It is documented that this}
7081 \textcolor{comment}{  happens. In earlier versions, the whole set of potential capturing offsets}
7082 \textcolor{comment}{  was set to -1 each time round the loop, but this is handled differently now.}
7083 \textcolor{comment}{  "Gaps" are set to -1 dynamically instead (this fixes a bug). Thus, it is only}
7084 \textcolor{comment}{  those at the end that need unsetting here. We can't just unset them all at}
7085 \textcolor{comment}{  the start of the whole thing because they may get set in one branch that is}
7086 \textcolor{comment}{  not the final matching branch. */}
7087 
7088   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a6befbc845fc277e998e3a29ec7868049}{end\_offset\_top}/2 <= re->top\_bracket && \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_afeda8db30b411d6c918c917b867d0309}{offsets} != 
      \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL})
7089     \{
7090     \textcolor{keyword}{register} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *iptr, *iend;
7091     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} resetcount = 2 + re->top\_bracket * 2;
7092     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (resetcount > offsetcount) resetcount = offsetcount;
7093     iptr = \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_afeda8db30b411d6c918c917b867d0309}{offsets} + md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a6befbc845fc277e998e3a29ec7868049}{end\_offset\_top};
7094     iend = \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_afeda8db30b411d6c918c917b867d0309}{offsets} + resetcount;
7095     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (iptr < iend) *iptr++ = -1;
7096     \}
7097 
7098   \textcolor{comment}{/* If there is space, set up the whole thing as substring 0. The value of}
7099 \textcolor{comment}{  md->start\_match\_ptr might be modified if \(\backslash\)K was encountered on the success}
7100 \textcolor{comment}{  matching path. */}
7101 
7102   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (offsetcount < 2) rc = 0; \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}
7103     \{
7104     \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_afeda8db30b411d6c918c917b867d0309}{offsets}[0] = (\hyperlink{group__MOD__WATCHDOG_gaf0b5a943e734de7ea24142e2c81d82ef}{int})(md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_a169aeb315352d6fffadb69076e89feff}{start\_match\_ptr} - md->
      \hyperlink{structmatch__data_a463372ba613f0f74066c89590b55f35e}{start\_subject});
7105     \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_afeda8db30b411d6c918c917b867d0309}{offsets}[1] = (\hyperlink{group__MOD__WATCHDOG_gaf0b5a943e734de7ea24142e2c81d82ef}{int})(md->\hyperlink{structmatch__data_aa6674b6c308e01247dcca159a137bbd8}{end\_match\_ptr} - md->
      \hyperlink{structmatch__data_a463372ba613f0f74066c89590b55f35e}{start\_subject});
7106     \}
7107 
7108   \textcolor{comment}{/* Return MARK data if requested */}
7109 
7110   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (extra\_data != \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL} && (extra\_data->flags & \hyperlink{pcre_8h_aaa0700c4e5ae62a2b7945d6aff00d7a3}{PCRE\_EXTRA\_MARK}) != 0)

7114   release\_match\_heapframes(&frame\_zero);
7115 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
7116   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__CONFIG_ga2e051c0ce9ee165170cd7973f2464512}{rc};
7117   \}
7118 
7119 \textcolor{comment}{/* Control gets here if there has been an error, or if the overall match}
7120 \textcolor{comment}{attempt has failed at all permitted starting positions. */}
7121 
7122 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (using\_temporary\_offsets)
7123   \{
7124   \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a927243fe3d588e31de3f3badd5c47d47}{DPRINTF}((\textcolor{stringliteral}{"Freeing temporary memory\(\backslash\)n"}));

7126   \}
7127 
7128 \textcolor{comment}{/* For anything other than nomatch or partial match, just return the code. */}
7129 
7130 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rc != \hyperlink{pcre__exec_8c_aca955f0e1e921adb03901b56eeff3da0}{MATCH\_NOMATCH} && rc != \hyperlink{pcre_8h_a15e18e8cc2d40840786a650ee750d49a}{PCRE\_ERROR\_PARTIAL})

7134   release\_match\_heapframes(&frame\_zero);
7135 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
7136   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__CONFIG_ga2e051c0ce9ee165170cd7973f2464512}{rc};
7137   \}
7138 
7139 \textcolor{comment}{/* Handle partial matches - disable any mark data */}
7140 
7141 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (match\_partial != \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL})
7142   \{

7151     \}

7154 
7155 \textcolor{comment}{/* This is the classic nomatch case */}
7156

7164

7169 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
7170 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__CONFIG_ga2e051c0ce9ee165170cd7973f2464512}{rc};
7171 \}

130 \textcolor{comment}{/* Finally, the character type table. In this, we used to exclude VT from the}
131 \textcolor{comment}{white space chars, because Perl didn't recognize it as such for \(\backslash\)s and for}
132 \textcolor{comment}{comments within regexes. However, Perl changed at release 5.18, so PCRE changed}
133 \textcolor{comment}{at release 8.34. */}
134 
135 \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 256; i++)
136   \{
137   \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} \hyperlink{group__MOD__PROXY_gaa51afdb6d96b938b938dc9439be201be}{x} = 0;
138   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (isspace(i)) x += \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a65dc078d774490ba90c0d33d3fdece35}{ctype\_space};

140   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (isdigit(i)) x += \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a3d4364a50c8029c795b0e0a0e7ca7fbd}{ctype\_digit};
141   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (isxdigit(i)) x += \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a3664754fb10bf65932bf8f0c8ed543ce}{ctype\_xdigit};
142   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{README_8txt_a25d7dd05239df8ce57a8921c43397d07}{isalnum}(i) || i == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\_'}) x += \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a442a60d2ab94f56f28e04ab175faf43f}{ctype\_word};
143 
144   \textcolor{comment}{/* Note: strchr includes the terminating zero in the characters it considers.}
145 \textcolor{comment}{  In this instance, that is ok because we want binary zero to be flagged as a}
146 \textcolor{comment}{  meta-character, which in this sense is any character that terminates a run}
147 \textcolor{comment}{  of data characters. */}
148 
149   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (strchr(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)*+?\{^.$|()["}, i) != 0) x += \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_af254c479da59731eb98c178ba2db0430}{ctype\_meta};
150   *p++ = \hyperlink{group__MOD__PROXY_gaa51afdb6d96b938b938dc9439be201be}{x};
151   \}
152 
153 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} yield;
154 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

265     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (utf) utf16\_char = \hyperlink{group__MOD__SSL__PRIVATE_gaa8cecfc5c5c054d2875c03e77b7be15d}{TRUE};
266 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
267     \textcolor{comment}{/* Fall through. */}
268 
269     \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:
270     length = \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_ae497efaa9e3ed86a5dd1ffc13991e81d}{PRIV}(OP\_lengths)[*\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__DAEMON_gaad7fdd8e91a6edc850f20f2fede630a9}{ptr}] - 1;
271     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
272 
273     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a157d5577a5b2f5986037d0d09c7dc77da1f99e671caee687d352cce89c95e04c9}{OP\_CLASS}:
274     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a157d5577a5b2f5986037d0d09c7dc77da73f1f5998cb564a4df3d4424f44fa974}{OP\_NCLASS}:
275     \textcolor{comment}{/* Skip the character bit map. */}
276     ptr += 32/\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a9d8efd0ad5b191db2a1793268600deb9}{pcre\_uchar});
277     length = 0;
278     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
279 
280     \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a157d5577a5b2f5986037d0d09c7dc77dacd62821c239c3917560a909bb19bceb3}{OP\_XCLASS}:
281     \textcolor{comment}{/* Reverse the size of the XCLASS instance. */}
282     ptr++;
283 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if defined COMPILE\_PCRE16}
284     *ptr = swap\_uint16(*ptr);
285 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#elif defined COMPILE\_PCRE32}
286     *ptr = swap\_uint32(*ptr);
287 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
288 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifndef COMPILE\_PCRE32}
289     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (\hyperlink{config_8h_a563fd7a205c425b3d546639ee71070ce}{LINK\_SIZE} > 1)
290       \{
291       \textcolor{comment}{/* LINK\_SIZE can be 1 or 2 in 16 bit mode. */}
292       ptr++;
293       *ptr = swap\_uint16(*ptr);
294       \}
295 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
296     ptr++;
297     length = (\hyperlink{group__MOD__PROXY_gga4e8622ade6bde29385df7b89c9b94e71a12a8dcf59c16b5aadfda3a08ba67d529}{GET}(ptr, -\hyperlink{config_8h_a563fd7a205c425b3d546639ee71070ce}{LINK\_SIZE})) - (1 + \hyperlink{config_8h_a563fd7a205c425b3d546639ee71070ce}{LINK\_SIZE} + 1);
298 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if defined COMPILE\_PCRE16}
299     *ptr = swap\_uint16(*ptr);
300 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#elif defined COMPILE\_PCRE32}
301     *ptr = swap\_uint32(*ptr);
302 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
303     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((*ptr & \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_ae1fdbc9124ca5c922fe49dbcb07ac9c0}{XCL\_MAP}) != 0)
304       \{
305       \textcolor{comment}{/* Skip the character bit map. */}
306       ptr += 32/\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a9d8efd0ad5b191db2a1793268600deb9}{pcre\_uchar});
307       length -= 32/\textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a9d8efd0ad5b191db2a1793268600deb9}{pcre\_uchar});
308       \}
309     \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};
310     \}
311   ptr++;
312   \}
313 \textcolor{comment}{/* Control should never reach here in 16/32 bit mode. */}
314 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#else  }\textcolor{comment}{/* In 8-bit mode, the pattern does not need to be processed. */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}
315 \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} 0;
316 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif }\textcolor{comment}{/* !COMPILE\_PCRE8 */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{}
317 \}
\end{DoxyCode}

1604     printf(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"Start bits:\(\backslash\)n"});
1605     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < 32; i++)
1606       printf(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"%3d: %02x%s"}, i * 8, *ptr++, ((i + 1) & 0x7) != 0? \textcolor{stringliteral}{" "} : \textcolor{stringliteral}{"\(\backslash\)n"});
1607     \}
1608 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#endif}
1609 
1610   \textcolor{comment}{/* Always set the minlength value in the block, because the JIT compiler}
1611 \textcolor{comment}{  makes use of it. However, don't set the bit unless the length is greater than}
1612 \textcolor{comment}{  zero - the interpretive pcre\_exec() and pcre\_dfa\_exec() needn't waste time}
1613 \textcolor{comment}{  checking the zero case. */}
1614 
1615   \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (min > 0)
1616     \{
1617     study->\hyperlink{structpcre__study__data_aa7f0cd71352343074202364478c25a4d}{flags} |= \hyperlink{pcre__internal_8h_a99cb4a3ffaa73a220e660acb23c749c4}{PCRE\_STUDY\_MINLEN};
1618     study->\hyperlink{structpcre__study__data_a50cb4fc8a227db9bfe3568764aca3274}{minlength} = \hyperlink{apr__random_8c_ac6afabdc09a49a433ee19d8a9486056d}{min};
1619     \}
1620   \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} study->\hyperlink{structpcre__study__data_a50cb4fc8a227db9bfe3568764aca3274}{minlength} = 0;
1621 
1622   \textcolor{comment}{/* If JIT support was compiled and requested, attempt the JIT compilation.}
1623 \textcolor{comment}{  If no starting bytes were found, and the minimum length is zero, and JIT}
1624 \textcolor{comment}{  compilation fails, abandon the extra block and return NULL, unless}
1625 \textcolor{comment}{  PCRE\_STUDY\_EXTRA\_NEEDED is set. */}
1626 
1627 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#ifdef SUPPORT\_JIT}
1628   extra->executable\_jit = \hyperlink{pcre_8txt_ad7f989d16aa8ca809a36bc392c07fba1}{NULL};

1635

1637       (\hyperlink{group__APACHE__CORE__MUTEX_gaa6c9d809037676d22aceaf5517a33faf}{options} & \hyperlink{pcre_8h_a0e994164f895575ba3ec61ef8af4c8e1}{PCRE\_STUDY\_EXTRA\_NEEDED}) == 0)
1638     \{
1639 \textcolor{preprocessor}{#if defined COMPILE\_PCRE8}

1647     \}

1650
